<div id="review_474656724" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/474656724" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474656724?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=like-a-virgin">like-a-virgin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474656724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8513173576731935319"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/>I have to admit that in my opinion Nalini Singh can't write a bad book. They all come in various degrees of good and awesome. This one was a "great" for me. Not awesome but better than just good. If I didn't want to distinguish the books in this series that I liked more than the others it would be a 5.<br/><br/>The reason this book wasn't a solid 5 for me was that I couldn't see when the romance began. It's like we begin reading and the heroes are already halfway there. This steals something fro</span>
  <span id="freeText8513173576731935319" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br /><br />I have to admit that in my opinion Nalini Singh can't write a bad book. They all come in various degrees of good and awesome. This one was a "great" for me. Not awesome but better than just good. If I didn't want to distinguish the books in this series that I liked more than the others it would be a 5.<br /><br />The reason this book wasn't a solid 5 for me was that I couldn't see when the romance began. It's like we begin reading and the heroes are already halfway there. This steals something from me. I want to be able to see the connection forming.<br /><br />Other than that the book was just as beautiful as any of Nalini's. Good writing, interesting characters, arresting story. I love how the author keeps building the feud between the Psy Council and the changelings and I like the fact that she keeps giving us glimpses in the lives of the previous couples. <br /><br />It is a rare book that can keep you enthralled for the second or third time you read it.<br /><br /><b>2nd re-read 4/9/2014</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8513173576731935319" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2320689592" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2320689592" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2320689592?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=v-card">v-card</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2320689592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14090545977250715220">4.25 Ice Baby Stars<br/><br/>I’m so glad I stuck to this series. I was really disappointed with the previous one, but Caressed by Ice was totally worth it.<br/><br/>Each books are a standalone, but to be honest the storyline is so complicated, I highly suggest you read them in order. I can’t even fully explain how everything works in this world, but I like reading it!<br/><br/>This series are a slow burn series with a lot of character development so don’t think you will get a lot of steam, but when you do it means something.</span>
  <span id="freeText14090545977250715220" style="display:none">4.25 Ice Baby Stars<br /><br />I’m so glad I stuck to this series. I was really disappointed with the previous one, but Caressed by Ice was totally worth it.<br /><br />Each books are a standalone, but to be honest the storyline is so complicated, I highly suggest you read them in order. I can’t even fully explain how everything works in this world, but I like reading it!<br /><br />This series are a slow burn series with a lot of character development so don’t think you will get a lot of steam, but when you do it means something. <br /><br />Brenna is the girl that was saved. She’s really messed up and you can’t help but feel for the girl. She was mentally raped and ready to move forward with her life.<br /><br />Judd seems to be the only man that can help calm Brenna, the only thing is, every time he feels a physical emotion towards Brenna, he physically hurts. Judd is a complicated character and it’s not easy to understand what is wrong with him. All I know is that he can’t physically be with Brenna and he tries very hard to push her away.<br /><br />I usually don’t like it when the Heroine chases after the guy but in this one I really loved it. The great thing about this author is that she doesn’t tell me how to feel towards the character I just do. I love Judd, he’s so complicated and I love how emotionless he is. He cares for Brenna, but he doesn’t show it and I love how he keeps on pushing her away. I really do!<br /><br />Of course there is a lot of politics. Who is after Brenna and what is the Psy council planning to do? I was kept on the edge of my seat the entire read and I read this in almost one sitting. I’m so glad I sucked to the series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14090545977250715220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_69795932" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/69795932" />
    <a title="Adrienne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2087365-adrienne"><img alt="Adrienne" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/69795932?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adrienne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adrienne" href="/user/show/2087365-adrienne">Adrienne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer69795932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3156098142284436615">One of my favourite books in the Psy-Changeling saga. This is the story of Judd (so Psy his got control on his control (also known as silence after the effect it has on silencing emotions)) and Brenna (damaged Snowdancer changeling). Besides the story between these two the empire that is the Psy world continues to develop, in this the third book. <br/><br/>Well, I was sucked in from the start and the thing I really like about this book is with every turn of the page something happens to keep you invested </span>
  <span id="freeText3156098142284436615" style="display:none">One of my favourite books in the Psy-Changeling saga. This is the story of Judd (so Psy his got control on his control (also known as silence after the effect it has on silencing emotions)) and Brenna (damaged Snowdancer changeling). Besides the story between these two the empire that is the Psy world continues to develop, in this the third book. <br /><br />Well, I was sucked in from the start and the thing I really like about this book is with every turn of the page something happens to keep you invested in the story, if it's not the incredible emotional (read sexual) tension between Judd ,who has been so locked into Silence that you really do wonder whether he can ever break free, and Brenna, who altho damaged by a Psy of the same designator as Judd, understands that there is something fundementally different about him, then it's the developing structure and politics taking place between the Psy Council.<br /><br />It's really difficult to write a review for this without giving any spoilers as every part of this story is interwoven, from the Psy councils underhand attempts to cause chaos within the Changeling world to Judds secret life outside the Snowdancers Den.<br /><br />The empire aside, Judd and Brenna are a perfect couple, Brenna recognizes that Judd is something more to her than a cold emotionless Psy and despite his reservations, in part due to the fact that his mind has been so cruelly conditioned to attack itself at the slightest hint of emotion Judd 'knows' the Brenna means something to him. As they come to understand the special relationship between them so Judds control starts to slide and in the moments when the control has slipped sufficient for him to think he realizes that there maybe a way forward. What follows could kill him but Judd takes the chance anyway, but will it be sufficient for Brenna who needs to 'find' a lost part of her being and also form a bond with Judd the love of her life? <br /><br />The between the sheets scenes are slow in coming due to the incredible control 'silence' places on Judd , but when they do happen my goodness the pages sizzle with love, you could say the earth moves literally:) <br /><br />This series ia a great read for anyone wanting more than just a romance story, the world created by Singh is multi layed and compelling to read about. I can't wait to read the next one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3156098142284436615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7589909781666918095">Oh nice, thank you Kindle! Book one in my "let's hide the cover of this novel so I can read it in public" went pretty well actually. I don't pretend that these books aren't racy lady reads, but for some reason this author's storytelling doesn't get old like the other authors in this genre. The world is pretty interesting, and although the romance stuff is pretty "see it a mile away" that's what these books are, and the fact that I'm still reading them I think is a testament to the quality of the</span>
  <span id="freeText7589909781666918095" style="display:none">Oh nice, thank you Kindle! Book one in my "let's hide the cover of this novel so I can read it in public" went pretty well actually. I don't pretend that these books aren't racy lady reads, but for some reason this author's storytelling doesn't get old like the other authors in this genre. The world is pretty interesting, and although the romance stuff is pretty "see it a mile away" that's what these books are, and the fact that I'm still reading them I think is a testament to the quality of the writing. I really enjoyed this in a TOTAL GUILTY PLEASURE WAY!<br />Of course, when ppl look at my Kindle and see "Caressed By Ice" in the main menu, it's not much less embarassing than the cover art. Well...ya it is :D</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HGmxIbWmdGBA8cbNq7KN9TpzF+gMqG9R23PYkVgVNQ1iPpX1zjHbqb9D8hMf6C9bbGsrrS+GHbXfgSSBmjGPaw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/71688.Nalini_Singh">About Nalini Singh</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3545397778229867252">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText3545397778229867252" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
